   82 00000000         ;---------------------------------------------------------------
   83 00000000         ;UART0_BDH
   84 00000000         ;    0->  7:LIN break detect IE (disabled)
   85 00000000         ;    0->  6:RxD input active edge IE (disabled)
   86 00000000         ;    0->  5:Stop bit number select (1)
   87 00000000         ;00001->4-0:SBR[12:0] (UART0CLK / [9600 * (OSR + 1)]) 
   88 00000000         ;UART0CLK is MCGFLLCLK
   89 00000000         ;MCGPLLCLK is 47972352 Hz ~=~ 48 MHz
   90 00000000         ;SBR ~=~ 48 MHz / (9600 * 16) = 312.5 --> 312 = 0x138
   91 00000000         ;SBR = 47972352 / (9600 * 16) = 312.32 --> 312 = 0x138
   92 00000000 00000001 
                       UART0_BDH_9600

                       UART0_BDL_9600
                               EQU              0x38
  101 00000000         ;---------------------------------------------------------------
  102 00000000         ;UART0_C1
  103 00000000         ;0-->7:LOOPS=loops select (normal)
  104 00000000         ;0-->6:DOZEEN=doze enable (disabled)
  105 00000000         ;0-->5:RSRC=receiver source select (internal--no effect LOOPS=0)
  106 00000000         ;0-->4:M=9- or 8-bit mode select 
  107 00000000         ;        (1 start, 8 data [lsb first], 1 stop)
  108 00000000         ;0-->3:WAKE=receiver wakeup method select (idle)
  109 00000000         ;0-->2:IDLE=idle line type select (idle begins after start bit)
  110 00000000         ;0-->1:PE=parity enable (disabled)
  111 00000000         ;0-->0:PT=parity type (even parity--no effect PE=0)
  112 00000000 00000000 
                       UART0_C1_8N1
                               EQU              0x00
  113 00000000         ;---------------------------------------------------------------
  114 00000000         ;UART0_C2
  115 00000000         ;0-->7:TIE=transmit IE for TDRE (disabled)
  116 00000000         ;0-->6:TCIE=transmission complete IE for TC (disabled)
  117 00000000         ;0-->5:RIE=receiver IE for RDRF (disabled)
  118 00000000         ;0-->4:ILIE=idle line IE for IDLE (disabled)
  119 00000000         ;1-->3:TE=transmitter enable (enabled)
  120 00000000         ;1-->2:RE=receiver enable (enabled)
  121 00000000         ;0-->1:RWU=receiver wakeup control (normal)
  122 00000000         ;0-->0:SBK=send break (disabled, normal)
  123 00000000 0000000C 
                       UART0_C2_T_R
                               EQU              (UART0_C2_TE_MASK :OR: UART0_C2_RE_MASK)
  124 00000000         ;---------------------------------------------------------------
  125 00000000         ;UART0_C3
  126 00000000         ;0-->7:R8T9=9th data bit for receiver (not used M=0)
  127 00000000         ;           10th data bit for transmitter (not used M10=0)
  128 00000000         ;0-->6:R9T8=9th data bit for transmitter (not used M=0)
  129 00000000         ;           10th data bit for receiver (not used M10=0)
  130 00000000         ;0-->5:TXDIR=UART_TX pin direction in single-wire mode
  131 00000000         ;            (no effect LOOPS=0)
  132 00000000         ;0-->4:TXINV=transmit data inversion (not inverted)
  133 00000000         ;0-->3:ORIE=overrun IE for OR (disabled)

ARM Macro Assembler    Page 11 Exercise 7 Circular FIFO Queue Operations


  376 00000100         
  377 00000100 684B            LDR              R3, [R1, #OUT_PTR]
  378 00000102         P_NEXT
  379 00000102         ;end of buffer reached
  380 00000102 2A00            CMP              R2, #0
  381 00000104 D00D            BEQ              P_EXIT
  382 00000106         
  383 00000106         ;print queue character
  384 00000106 781C            LDRB             R4, [R3, #0]
  385 00000108         
  386 00000108         ;Move char to R0 to print
  387 00000108 B401            PUSH             {R0}
  388 0000010A 0020            MOVS             R0, R4
  389 0000010C F7FF FFFE       BL               PutChar
  390 00000110 BC01            POP              {R0}
  391 00000112         
  392 00000112         ;Decrement num_enqd
  393 00000112 1E52            SUBS             R2, R2, #1
  394 00000114         
  395 00000114         ;Increment the out_ptr
  396 00000114 1C5B            ADDS             R3, R3, #1
  397 00000116         
  398 00000116         ;Compare OUT_PTR to BUF_PAST
  399 00000116         ;If out_ptr >= BUF_PAST, wrap the queue around
  400 00000116 68CC            LDR              R4, [R1, #BUF_PAST]
  401 00000118 42A3            CMP              R3, R4
  402 0000011A D000            BEQ              P_WRAP
  403 0000011C         
  404 0000011C E7F1            B                P_NEXT
  405 0000011E         
  406 0000011E         P_WRAP
  407 0000011E         ;Adjust out_ptr to equal buf_strt
  408 0000011E         ;Thus wrapping around the circular queue
  409 0000011E 688B            LDR              R3, [R1, #BUF_STRT]
  410 00000120 E7EF            B                P_NEXT
  411 00000122         
  412 00000122         P_EXIT
  413 00000122         ;print delimiter

  534 000001B4         InitQueue
                               PROC             {R0-R14}
  535 000001B4         ;InitQueue: Initalize Circular FIFO Queue Structure
  536 000001B4         ;Inputs:
  537 000001B4         ; R0 - Memory location of queue buffer
  538 000001B4         ; R1 - Address to place Queue record structure
  539 000001B4         ; R2 - Size of queue structure (character capacity)
  540 000001B4         ;Outputs:
  541 000001B4         ; none
  542 000001B4         ;--------------------------------------------



ARM Macro Assembler    Page 15 Exercise 7 Circular FIFO Queue Operations


  543 000001B4 B407            PUSH             {R0-R2}
  544 000001B6         
  545 000001B6         
  546 000001B6         ;Store memory address of front of queue
  547 000001B6         ;Into IN_PTR position of the buffer
  548 000001B6 6008            STR              R0, [R1, #IN_PTR]
  549 000001B8         
  550 000001B8         ;Store same memory address for OUT_PTR
  551 000001B8         ;position in the buffer since queue is empty
  552 000001B8 6048            STR              R0, [R1, #OUT_PTR]
  553 000001BA         
  554 000001BA         ;Store same memory address in BUF_STRT for initalization
  555 000001BA 6088            STR              R0, [R1, #BUF_STRT]
  556 000001BC         
  557 000001BC         ;Store BUF_PAST in last slot of buffer
  558 000001BC 1880            ADDS             R0, R0, R2
  559 000001BE 60C8            STR              R0, [R1, #BUF_PAST]
  560 000001C0         
  561 000001C0         ;Store BUF_SIZE with size in R2
  562 000001C0 740A            STRB             R2, [R1, #BUF_SIZE]
  563 000001C2         
  564 000001C2         ;Initalize NUM_ENQD to zero and 
  565 000001C2         ;store in 6th slot of buffer
  566 000001C2 2000            MOVS             R0, #0
  567 000001C4 7448            STRB             R0, [R1, #NUM_ENQD]
  568 000001C6 BC07            POP              {R0-R2}
  569 000001C8 4770            BX               LR
  570 000001CA                 ENDP
  571 000001CA         ;**************************************    
  572 000001CA         
  573 000001CA         Dequeue PROC             {R1-R14}
  574 000001CA         ;Dequeue: Remove an element from the circular FIFO Queue
  575 000001CA         ;Inputs:
  576 000001CA         ; R1 - Address of Queue record structure
  577 000001CA         ;Outputs:
  578 000001CA         ; R0 - Character that has been dequeued
  579 000001CA         ; PSR C flag : Failure - C = 1
  580 000001CA         ;     Success - C = 0 
  581 000001CA         ;--------------------------------------------
  582 000001CA B41E            PUSH             {R1-R4}
  583 000001CC         
  584 000001CC         ;If the number enqueued is 0, 



ARM Macro Assembler    Page 16 Exercise 7 Circular FIFO Queue Operations


  585 000001CC         ;Set failure PSR flag
  586 000001CC 7C4B            LDRB             R3, [R1, #NUM_ENQD]
  587 000001CE 2B00            CMP              R3, #0
  588 000001D0 DD14            BLE              DEQUEUE_FAILURE
  589 000001D2         
  590 000001D2 684C            LDR              R4, [R1, #OUT_PTR]
  591 000001D4         
  592 000001D4         ;Remove the item from the queue
  593 000001D4         ;And place in R0
  594 000001D4 7820            LDRB             R0, [R4, #0]
  595 000001D6         
  596 000001D6         ;Decrement number of enqueued elements
  597 000001D6         ;And store info back in buffer
  598 000001D6 7C4B            LDRB             R3, [R1, #NUM_ENQD]
  599 000001D8 1E5B            SUBS             R3, R3, #1
  600 000001DA 744B            STRB             R3, [R1, #NUM_ENQD]
  601 000001DC         
  602 000001DC         
  603 000001DC         ;Increment location of out_pointer
  604 000001DC 1C64            ADDS             R4, R4, #1
  605 000001DE         
  606 000001DE         
  607 000001DE         ;Compare OUT_PTR to BUF_PAST
  608 000001DE         ;If out_ptr >= BUF_PAST, wrap the queue around
  609 000001DE 68CB            LDR              R3, [R1, #BUF_PAST]
  610 000001E0 42A3            CMP              R3, R4
  611 000001E2 D001            BEQ              WRAP_BUFFER
  612 000001E4         
  613 000001E4 604C            STR              R4, [R1, #OUT_PTR]
  614 000001E6 E001            B                DEQUEUE_CLEAR_PSR
  615 000001E8         
  616 000001E8         WRAP_BUFFER
  617 000001E8         ;Adjust out_ptr to equal buf_strt
  618 000001E8         ;Thus wrapping around the circular queue
  619 000001E8 688B            LDR              R3, [R1, #BUF_STRT]
  620 000001EA 604B            STR              R3, [R1, #OUT_PTR]
  621 000001EC         
  622 000001EC         DEQUEUE_CLEAR_PSR
  623 000001EC         ;Clear the PSR C flag
  624 000001EC F3EF 8100       MRS              R1, APSR
  625 000001F0 2320            MOVS             R3, #C_MASK
  626 000001F2 0609            LSLS             R1, R1, #C_SHIFT



ARM Macro Assembler    Page 17 Exercise 7 Circular FIFO Queue Operations


  627 000001F4 4399            BICS             R1, R1, R3
  628 000001F6 F381 8800       MSR              APSR, R1
  629 000001FA         
  630 000001FA         ;Successfully end the operation
  631 000001FA E006            B                END_DEQUEUE
  632 000001FC         
  633 000001FC         DEQUEUE_FAILURE
  634 000001FC         ;Set PSR C flag to 1
  635 000001FC F3EF 8100       MRS              R1, APSR
  636 00000200 2320            MOVS             R3, #C_MASK
  637 00000202 061B            LSLS             R3, R3, #C_SHIFT
  638 00000204 4319            ORRS             R1, R1, R3

  645 0000020E         ;**************************************   
  646 0000020E         
  647 0000020E         Enqueue PROC             {R0-R14}
  648 0000020E         ;Enqueue: Add an element to the circular FIFO Queue
  649 0000020E         ;Inputs:
  650 0000020E         ;R0 - Character to enqueue
  651 0000020E         ;R1 - Address of the Queue record
  652 0000020E         ;Outputs:
  653 0000020E         ;PSR C flag (failure if C = 1, C = 0 otherwise.)
  654 0000020E         ;--------------------------------------------'
  655 0000020E         
  656 0000020E B41C            PUSH             {R2, R3, R4}
  657 00000210         
  658 00000210         ;If num_enqd >= size of the queue
  659 00000210         ;Then set PSR C flag to 1 indicating
  660 00000210         ;the error that an element was not inserted
  661 00000210         ;into a full queue
  662 00000210

  664 00000212 7C0C            LDRB             R4, [R1, #BUF_SIZE]

  666 00000216 DA00            BGE              QUEUE_FULL
  667 00000218 E007            B                BEGIN_ENQUEUE
  668 0000021A         



ARM Macro Assembler    Page 18 Exercise 7 Circular FIFO Queue Operations


  669 0000021A         QUEUE_FULL
  670 0000021A         ;Set PSR C flag to 1
  671 0000021A F3EF 8100       MRS              R1, APSR
  672 0000021E 2320            MOVS             R3, #C_MASK
  673 00000220 061B            LSLS             R3, R3, #C_SHIFT
  674 00000222 4319            ORRS             R1, R1, R3

  676 00000228 E01B            B                END_ENQUEUE
  677 0000022A         
  678 0000022A         BEGIN_ENQUEUE
  679 0000022A         
  680 0000022A         ;Load mem address of in_ptr
  681 0000022A         ;and then store the value to be enqueued
  682 0000022A         ;into the value at that memory address
  683 0000022A 680B            LDR              R3, [R1, #IN_PTR]
  684 0000022C 7018            STRB             R0, [R3, #0]
  685 0000022E

  687 0000022E         ;The queue item. Then store back in IN_PTR

  693 00000232

  696 00000234 1C5B            ADDS             R3, R3, #1

  698 00000238

  700 00000238         ;Loop around and adjust inPtr to beginning of
  701 00000238         ;the queue buffer

  703 0000023A 68CC            LDR              R4, [R1, #BUF_PAST]

  892 0000030C         GetChar PROC             {R1-R14}
  893 0000030C         ;/* Output:  R0:  Character received */
  894 0000030C         ; repeat 
  895 0000030C         ;      {check RDRF bit of UART0_S1
  896 0000030C         ;   }until (RDRF= 1)
  897 0000030C         ; get character received from UART0_D
  898 0000030C         ; return }
  899 0000030C B40E            PUSH             {R1, R2, R3} ;Register retention
  900 0000030E         
  901 0000030E 4969            LDR              R1, =UART0_BASE

 1087 000003B6         DIVU    PROC             {R2-R14}
 1088 000003B6         ;****************************************************************
 1089 000003B6         ; Performs the division operation upon R1 by dividing it from R0
 1090 000003B6         ; and returning the Quotient and Remainder in R0 and R1 
 1091 000003B6         ; respectively. If Division by 0 is top be performed, R0 and R1 
 1092 000003B6         ; do not change their values, instead C bit is set.
 1093 000003B6         ;
 1094 000003B6         ; R0 rem R1 = R1 / R0 
 1095 000003B6         ;****************************************************************
 1096 000003B6 B40C            PUSH             {R2-R3}     ;Temporary Registers  
 1097 000003B8 2800            CMP              R0, #0      ;Check for division by 0
 1098 000003BA D014            BEQ              DIV_BY_0
 1099 000003BC 2900            CMP              R1, #0      ;Check for division of 0   
 1100 000003BE D00F            BEQ              DIV_OF_0
 1101 000003C0         
 1102 000003C0 0002            MOVS             R2, R0      ;Temporarily storing the dividend
 1103 000003C2 2000            MOVS             R0, #0      ;Initializing the quotient
 1104 000003C4         
 1105 000003C4 4291    While   CMP              R1,R2       ;check for Dividend >= Divisor
 1106 000003C6 D302            BLO              DIV_END
 1107 000003C8 1A89            SUBS             R1,R1,R2    ;Dividend -= Divisor
 1108 000003CA 1C40            ADDS             R0,R0,#1    ;Quotient++
 1109 000003CC E7FA            B                While
 1110 000003CE         
 1111 000003CE F3EF 8200 
                       DIV_END MRS              R2, APSR    ;Clear flags.
 1112 000003D2 2320            MOVS             R3, #C_MASK ;Create Mask
 1113 000003D4 061B            LSLS             R3,R3,#C_SHIFT ;Shift to MSB
 1114 000003D6 439A            BICS             R2,R3       ;
 1115 000003D8 F382 8800       MSR              APSR, R2
 1116 000003DC         
 1117 000003DC BC0C    DIV_DONE
                               POP              {R2-R3}     ;Store Temporary Registers.
 1118 000003DE 4770            BX               LR
 1119 000003E0         
 1120 000003E0 2000    DIV_OF_0
                               MOVS             R0, #0      ;Set Quotient = 0
 1121 000003E2 2100            MOVS             R1, #0      ;Set Remainder = 0
